### kaggle地址

[房价预测问题](https://www.kaggle.com/c/house-prices-advanced-regression-techniques)

### 1. 读取csv数据

```{.python .input  n=1}
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd

train_data = pd.read_csv('train.csv')
test_data = pd.read_csv('test.csv')
```

对连续特征的Nan值，使用均值代替

```{.python .input  n=10}
all_x = all_x.fillna(all_x.mean())
```

分解得到预处理完成的数据，转化为训练所需的数据

```{.python .input  n=11}
import mxnet.ndarray as nd

seq_row = train_data.shape[0]
train_x = all_x[:seq_row].as_matrix()
test_x = all_x[seq_row:].as_matrix()
train_y = train_data.SalePrice.as_matrix()

X_train = nd.array(train_x)
y_train = nd.array(train_y)
y_train.reshape((seq_row, 1))
X_test = nd.array(test_x)
```

### 4. 定义回归模型

```{.python .input  n=42}
from mxnet import gluon

def get_net():
    net = gluon.nn.Sequential()
    with net.name_scope():
        net.add(gluon.nn.Dense(200, activation="relu"))
        net.add(gluon.nn.Dense(1))
    net.initialize()
    return net
```

### 5. 训练

```{.python .input  n=36}
import mxnet as mx
import mxnet.autograd as ag
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

square_loss = gluon.loss.HuberLoss()
# square_loss = gluon.loss.L2Loss()

def get_rmse_log(net, X_train, y_train):
    num_train = X_train.shape[0]
    clipped_preds = nd.clip(net(X_train), 1, float('inf'))
    return np.sqrt(2 * nd.sum(square_loss(nd.log(clipped_preds), nd.log(y_train))).asscalar() / num_train)

def training(net, cost_fun, x_data, y_data, x_test, y_test, epochs, batch_size, learning_rate, weight_decay):
    train_loss = []
    test_loss = []
    dataset_train = gluon.data.ArrayDataset(x_data, y_data)
    data_iter = gluon.data.DataLoader(dataset_train, batch_size, shuffle=True) 
    trainer = gluon.Trainer(net.collect_params(), 'Adam', {'learning_rate': learning_rate,'wd': weight_decay})
    net.collect_params().initialize(force_reinit=True)
    for epoch in range(epochs):
        for data, label in data_iter:
            with ag.record():
                yhat = net(data)
                loss = square_loss(yhat, label)
            loss.backward()
            trainer.step(batch_size)
        cur_train_loss = get_rmse_log(net, x_data, y_data)
        if epoch > epochs-5:
            print("Epoch %d, train loss: %f" % (epoch, cur_train_loss))
        train_loss.append(cur_train_loss)
        if x_test is not None:    
            cur_test_loss = get_rmse_log(net, x_test, y_test)
            test_loss.append(cur_test_loss)
    plt.plot(train_loss)
    plt.legend(['train'])
    if X_test is not None:
        plt.plot(test_loss)
        plt.legend(['train','test'])
    plt.show()
    if x_test is not None:
        return cur_train_loss, cur_test_loss
    else:
        return cur_train_loss
```

### 6. K折交叉验证（选模型）

K折交叉验证，官方向导文件源码看了半天都不知道是选择最优的参数的，结果查了半天，才发现它是用来选择模型而不是用来选择参数的......

```{.python .input  n=45}
import matplotlib as mpl
mpl.rcParams['figure.dpi']= 120

def k_fold_cross_valid(k, epochs, X_train, y_train, learning_rate, weight_decay):
    assert k > 1
    fold_size = X_train.shape[0] // k
    train_loss_sum = 0.0
    test_loss_sum = 0.0
    for test_i in range(k):
        X_val_test = X_train[test_i * fold_size: (test_i + 1) * fold_size, :]
        y_val_test = y_train[test_i * fold_size: (test_i + 1) * fold_size]

        val_train_defined = False
        for i in range(k):
            if i != test_i:
                X_cur_fold = X_train[i * fold_size: (i + 1) * fold_size, :]
                y_cur_fold = y_train[i * fold_size: (i + 1) * fold_size]
                if not val_train_defined:
                    X_val_train = X_cur_fold
                    y_val_train = y_cur_fold
                    val_train_defined = True
                else:
                    X_val_train = nd.concat(X_val_train, X_cur_fold, dim=0)
                    y_val_train = nd.concat(y_val_train, y_cur_fold, dim=0)
        net = get_net() 
        train_loss, test_loss = training(net, square_loss, X_val_train, y_val_train, X_val_test, y_val_test,
                                         epochs, 100, learning_rate, weight_decay)
        train_loss_sum += train_loss
        print("Test loss: %f \n" % test_loss)
        test_loss_sum += test_loss
    return train_loss_sum / k, test_loss_sum / k

k = 5
epochs = 100
learning_rate = 0.1
weight_decay = 0.01
train_loss, test_loss = k_fold_cross_valid(k, epochs, X_train,
                                           y_train, learning_rate, weight_decay)
print("%d-fold validation: Avg train loss: %f, Avg test loss: %f" %
      (k, train_loss, test_loss))
```

### 7. 使用选好的模型进行预测

```{.python .input  n=15}
def learn(epochs, X_train, y_train, test, learning_rate, weight_decay):
    net = get_net()
    training(net, square_loss, X_train, y_train, None, None, epochs, 100, learning_rate, weight_decay)
    preds = net(X_test).asnumpy()
    test['SalePrice'] = pd.Series(preds.reshape(1, -1)[0])
    submission = pd.concat([test['Id'], test['SalePrice']], axis=1)
    submission.to_csv('submission.csv', index=False)  
```

```{.python .input  n=16}
learn(epochs, X_train, y_train, test_data, learning_rate, weight_decay)
```
